name:Tâ€hâ€eâ€Tâ€râ€aâ€vâ€eâ€lâ€Sâ€hâ€oâ€w
info:Superior Double Room
info:Stayed in December 2022
info:Friends
info:17 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted December 12, 2022
msg:Located next to the river in Baise, this hotel sits on a quiet street and driveway, away from traffic. The hotel has gardens and also the interesting Red Sprit Park is behind the hotel too. There is a shopping mall that is about a 10-minute walk away and has various restaurants and shops. Likewise, all areas of the city are easy to reach, including the train station and the new main shopping area. 
The hotel boasts a SPA area that includes a good size swimming pool with good temperature water, gym and games rooms. There are also 2 restaurants-Chinese and Western. Check-in was swift, however the hotel is huge, so rooms can be a good 5-minute walk from the lobby itself. 
Rooms are very comfortable and the bed is nice and soft. The bathtub and ahowers are also excellent quality. Overall, a very good hotel and wouldn't hesitate coming back to stay again.
